preserue theyr foresaied chanelles defende theyr citee ioygne maine lande pthe banke rehersed broken vii place whiche botes maie come shippe passe uenice sauyng porte malamoco two castelles lio entrie emperours displeasure accompted selfe maner sure hym innocence restyng hym selfe certayne space genoa departed towardes lion fraunce helde generall counsaill agaynst emperour federike duryng whose life durste retourne italy immediately emperours death came backe againe genoa lesse triumphantly receiued first tyme death emperour genowaies also recouered saona dyuers townes emperours tyme rebelled theim dooen theim notable displeasure well sea lande bishop innocence beyng departed genoa milaine wrought banished mastarati restored theyr countrey againe poundes paied theim comminaltee recompence theyr goodes taken awaie longe people made commocion office potestate rumour ceasyng elected guglielmo bocanigra citesin theyr capitaine superiour vnto potestate magistrate beyng placed
